<script>
var def_tawk_bottom = "20px"; /*This is their default style that I want to change*/
var def_tawk_right = "6px"; /*This is their default style that I want to change*/
var customize_tawk = ""; /*Interval object*/

function customize_tawk_widget(){
    var cur_bottom = jQuery("iframe[title='chat widget']").eq(0).css('bottom'); /*Get the default style*/
    var cur_right = jQuery("iframe[title='chat widget']").eq(0).css('right'); /*Get the default style*/
    // if(cur_bottom == def_tawk_bottom && cur_right == def_tawk_right){
        /*Check if the default style exists then remove it and add my custom style*/
        jQuery("iframe[title='chat widget']").eq(0).css({ 'right': '5px', 'bottom': '79px' });
        // jQuery("iframe[title='chat widget']").eq(0).addClass("custom-chat-widget");
        clearInterval(customize_tawk);
    // }
}

/*Customize the widget as soon as the widget is loaded*/
Tawk_API = Tawk_API || {};
Tawk_API.onLoad = function(){
    /*Only for mobile version*/
    if(/android|webos|iphone|ipad|ipod|blackberry|iemobile|opera mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
        var customize_tawk = setInterval(customize_tawk_widget, 100);
    }
};

/*Customize the widget as soon as the widget is minimized*/
Tawk_API = Tawk_API || {};
Tawk_API.onChatMinimized = function(){
    /*Only for mobile version*/
    if(/android|webos|iphone|ipad|ipod|blackberry|iemobile|opera mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
        var customize_tawk = setInterval(customize_tawk_widget, 100);
    }
};

</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
  // Open modal when button is clicked
  $('#myModal').on('click', function() {
    $('#myModal').css('display', 'block');
  });

  // Close modal when clicked outside of it
  $(window).on('click', function(event) {
    if (event.target === $('#myModal')[0]) {
      location.reload(); // Reload the page
    }
  });
});
    
</script>




<script>
    $("#pay_type").change(function() {
          var value = $(this).val(); 
          // alert(value); 
          if(value == 'hdfc')
          {
            var trans_amt = document.getElementById("trnasec_amt").textContent;
            
            var conv_charge = '0';
            
            var payout_hdfc_type = 'fixed';
            
            
                if(payout_hdfc_type=='percentage')
                {
                conv_charge = conv_charge/100;
                
                var sum = 0;
                
                sum = parseInt(trans_amt) * conv_charge;
                
                //console.log(sum);
                
                sum = sum + parseInt(trans_amt);
                
                //console.log(sum);
                
                document.getElementById("amount_charge_text").innerHTML = sum;
                
                var txn=0;
                txn=sum;
                
                //console.log(txn);
                // alert(txn); 
                // document.getElementById("TXN_AMOUNT").value = txn;
                $('#TXN_AMOUNT').val(txn);
                }
                else
                {
                    var sum = 0;
                    sum = parseInt(trans_amt) +parseInt(conv_charge);
                    
                    //console.log(sum);
                    
                    document.getElementById("amount_charge_text").innerHTML = sum;
                    
                    var txn=0;
                    txn=sum;
                    
                    //console.log(txn);
                    // alert(txn);
                    
                    // document.getElementById("TXN_AMOUNT").value = txn;
                    $('#TXN_AMOUNT').val(txn);
                }
                
                
            
          }
          
          if(value=='Paytm')
          {
           //paytm code
            
          }
          
        });
    
</script>












<script>
  function send_data_paytm(){
      
    var type = document.getElementById("pay_type").value ;        

         var trnas_amt = document.getElementById("cost_modal");
          var t_amt =parseFloat(trnas_amt.value);
          

          var order_id = document.getElementById("order_id").value ;

          var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id").value ;
          
          var rem = document.getElementById("rem").value;
          
           var upiid = document.getElementById("upiid").value;
          
          var checkboxValue = document.getElementById("term").checked;
          
          
          
          
            //  if (t_amt>0 && type=='Paytm') {
            
              if ( type=='') { 
                alert('SELCT PAYMENT TYPE.');
              }
              else if(upiid=='')
              {
                   alert('Enter UPI ID');
              }
              else if(checkboxValue=='')
              {
                   alert('Select term and condition');
              }
              else if ( type=='hdfc') { 

                document.getElementById("TXN_AMOUNT").value = t_amt ;
                  // alert(t_amt);
              // document.getElementById("ORDER_ID").value = order_id + '~' + user_id ;
              document.getElementById("ORDER_ID").value = order_id  ;
              document.getElementById("CUST_ID").value = user_id ;
              save_form_paytm('hdfc') ;
                // sendData();
                  //exit();
              }

             else if ( type=='Paytm') {
              document.getElementById("TXN_AMOUNT").value = '1'; //t_amt

              // document.getElementById("ORDER_ID").value = order_id + '~' + user_id ;
              document.getElementById("ORDER_ID").value = order_id  ;
              document.getElementById("CUST_ID").value = user_id;

              
             
              // save_form_paytm('paytm') ;
             }
  }
</script>

<script>
    $("#pay_type").change(function() {
          var value = $(this).val(); 
          //alert(value); 
          if(value=='hdfc')
          {
           var element = document.getElementById("hdfc_sub");
            element.style.display = "block";
          }
          if(value=='Paytm')
          {
            var element = document.getElementById("hdfc_sub");
            element.style.display = "none";
            
          }


          
        });

<script>
    function sendData(){
      var type = document.getElementById("pay_type").value ;
        
         
          var trnas_amt = document.getElementById("trnasec_amt").textContent;
          
          var t_amt=parseInt(trnas_amt);
          
           var checkboxValue = document.getElementById("term").checked;  
           
           var rem = document.getElementById("rem").value;
           //alert(rem); 
         
         
            if (t_amt>0 && type=='hdfc' && checkboxValue == true) {
               //alert("trans save");
                var amt_charge = document.getElementById("amount_charge_text").textContent;
                t_amt=parseInt(amt_charge);
                
                var upiid = document.getElementById("upiid"); 
                var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id").value;
                var order_id = document.getElementById("order_id").value;
                var uid = document.getElementById("uid");
                var payer_name = upiid.value;
                var pgmerid = 'HDFC000022529749';
                //alert(user_id);
                    $.ajax({
                        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/hdfc_trans_amount_save',
                        type: 'POST',
                        data: { 
                        amount: t_amt, 
                        payer_name: payer_name,
                        pgmerid:pgmerid,
                        order_no:order_id,
                        id:user_id,
                        rem:rem
                        },
                        success: function(response) {
                        var data = JSON.parse(response);
                        var msg=data.msg;
                       if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                           //alert("sachin");
                           successData();
                        }
                        else{
                           var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('t_failed'), {
                                    keyboard: false,
		                            backdrop: 'static' 
                            });
                            paymentModal.show();
                             var tc_failed = document.getElementById("tc_failed"); 
                           tc_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                              location.reload();
                            });
                            
                        }
                      }
                    });
                
                
            }
            
            
                
    }
    
     function successData()
    {
        //alert('sachin');
       // var uid = document.getElementById("uid");
        //var uid = uid.value;

        var amt_charge = document.getElementById("amount_charge_text").textContent;
        var total_amt=parseInt(amt_charge);
        var upiid = document.getElementById("upiid"); 
        var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id").value;
        var order_id = document.getElementById("order_id").value;
        var payer_name = upiid.value;
        var pgmerid = 'HDFC000022529749';
                $.ajax({
                url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/hdfc_trans_collect_prod',
                type: 'POST',
                data: { 
                payer_name: payer_name,
                pgmerid:pgmerid,
                order_no:order_id,
                amount:total_amt,
                id:user_id
                },
                success: function(response) {
                console.log(response); 
                //exit();
                var data = JSON.parse(response);
                var msg=data.msg;
                var upi=data.upi;
                var orderno=data.orderno;
                var amt=data.amt;
                var vpaid=data.vpaid;
                var pg_id='HDFC000022529749';
               if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                   timer(300);
                    // Define a variable to store the interval
                    var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
                        $.ajax({
                            url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/hdfc_trans_status_prod',
                            type: 'POST',
                            data: { 
                                pg_id:pg_id,
                                orderno: orderno,
                                upi:upi,
                                user_id:user_id
                            },
                            success: function(response) {
                                console.log(response);
                                var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                var cust_ref_no=data.cust_ref_no;
                                var status=data.status;
                                if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval
                                    var timeout_close = document.getElementById("timeout"); 
                                    timeout_close.style.display = "none";
                                    var customer_Receipt = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('customer_Receipt'), {
                                        keyboard: false,
		                                backdrop: 'static' 
                                    });
                                    document.getElementById("msg").innerHTML = status;
                                    document.getElementById("upi_txn_no").innerHTML = upi;
                                    document.getElementById("order_no").innerHTML = orderno; 
                                    document.getElementById("t_amt").innerHTML = amt;
                                    document.getElementById("cust_ref_no").innerHTML = cust_ref_no;
                                    document.getElementById("vppaid").innerHTML = vpaid;
                                    customer_Receipt.show();
                                    $.ajax({
                                          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/update_success_table',
                                          type: 'POST',
                                          data: { 
                                            orderno: orderno,
                                            user_id:user_id,
                                            upi:upi,
                                            status:status
                                          },
                                          success: function(response) {
                                              console.log(response);
                                            var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                            if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                                                console.log("updated");
                                                var close_receipt = document.getElementById("close_receipt"); 
                                                close_receipt.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                                    var cong = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('cong'), {
                                                    keyboard: false,
		                                            backdrop: 'static' 
                                                });
                                                cong.show();
                                                 var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id").value;
                                                var order_id = document.getElementById("order_id").value;
                                                 document.getElementById("user_id_text").innerHTML = user_id; 
                                                document.getElementById("order_id_text").innerHTML = order_id;
                                                
                                                var string = order_id;
                                                var psa = 'PSA-JOIN';
                                                var pmjay = 'PMJ-JOIN';
                                                
                                                console.log(string.includes(psa)) ;
                                                console.log(string.includes(pmjay)) ;
                                                
                                                    if (  (string.includes(psa) ) || (string.includes(pmjay) ) ) {
                                                                 document.getElementById("div_user_password").style.display = "none";
                                                }else{
                                                     document.getElementById("div_user_password").style.display = "";
                                                }
                                                
                                                //
                                                });
                                                document.getElementById("myModal").style.display = "none";
                                                var close_cong = document.getElementById("close_cong"); 
                                                close_cong.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                                    location.reload();
                                                    
                                                });
                                                
                                                
                                                
                                            }
                                            else{
                                                console.log("not updated");
                                            }
                                          }
                                        });
                                        
                                        
                                    
                                    //
                                    var close_receipt = document.getElementById("close_receipt"); 
                                    close_receipt.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                        //location.reload();
                                        
                                    });
                                    
                                    
                                }
                                else if (data.status === 'REJECTED') {
                                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval
                                    var timeout_close = document.getElementById("timeout"); 
                                    timeout_close.style.display = "none";
                                    var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('trnas_failed'), {
                                       keyboard: false,
		                               backdrop: 'static' 
                                    });
                                    document.getElementById("fail_msg").innerHTML = status;

                                    paymentModal.show();

                                            user_id:user_id,
                                            upi:upi,
                                            status:status
                                          },

                                              console.log(response);
                                            var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                            if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                                                console.log("updated")
                                                document.getElementById("myModal").style.display = "none";
                                            }
                                            else{
                                                console.log("not updated")
                                            }
                                          }
                                        });  
                                        
                                        
                                    
                                    var close_failed = document.getElementById("close_failed"); 
                                    close_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                         location.reload();
                                       
                                    });
                                }
                                //
                                else if (data.status === 'FAILED') {
                                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval
                                    var timeout_close = document.getElementById("timeout"); 
                                    timeout_close.style.display = "none";
                                    var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('trnas_failed'), {
                                        keyboard: false,
		                                backdrop: 'static' 
                                    });
                                    document.getElementById("fail_msg").innerHTML = status;

                                    document.getElementById("vpaid").innerHTML = vpaid;

                                    $.ajax({
                                          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/update_rejected_table',
                                          type: 'POST',
                                          data: { 
                                            orderno: orderno,
                                            user_id:user_id,
                                            upi:upi,
                                            status:status

                                              console.log(response);

                                            if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {

                                    close_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                         location.reload();
                                       
                                    });
                                }  
                                
                                
                            //

                        });
                    }, 2000);
                   
                   
             //

            else{
               var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('trnas_collect_failed'), {

    function verVpa(val){
        //alert("verifyvpa");
        var a11 = document.getElementById("a11");
        var pay = document.getElementById("pay");
        
        var upiid = document.getElementById("upiid").value;
        var vpaid=val;
        var pg_id = document.getElementById("pg_id");
       var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id").value;
       var order_id = document.getElementById("order_id").value;
        //var pg_id = pg_id.value;
        var pg_id='HDFC000022529749';
        // alert(pg_id);
        var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/verify_vpaid';
        /*alert(ac);
        */
        $.ajax({
          url: ac,
          type: 'POST',
          data: { 
            vpaid: vpaid,
            pg_id:pg_id,
            user_id:user_id
          },
          success: function(response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            if (data.status === 'VE') {
                a11.style.display = "block";
                //document.getElementById("a11").innerHTML = "Verified";
               document.getElementById("a11").innerHTML='<img src="https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/assest/img/success.gif" style="width: 3rem; height: 3rem;" >';
                pay.disabled = false;
                document.getElementById("pay").disabled = false;
                
                
                /*var verify = document.getElementById("verify");
                 verify.style.display = "none";
                
                var verify_fail = document.getElementById("verify_fail");
                verify_fail.style.display = "none";
                
                var verify_success = document.getElementById("verify_success");
                verify_success.style.display = "block";*/
                 
                 
                
            }
            else{
                 a11.style.display = "block";
              //  document.getElementById('a11').style.color = 'red';
              //   document.getElementById('a11').style.backgroundColor = 'red';
                //document.getElementById("a11").innerHTML = "Not Verified";
                document.getElementById("a11").innerHTML = '<img src="https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/assest/img/failed.gif" style="width: 2rem; height: 2rem;">';
                pay.disabled = true;
                document.getElementById("pay").disabled = true;
                
                
                /*var verify = document.getElementById("verify");
                 verify.style.display = "none";
                 
                var verify_success = document.getElementById("verify_success");
                verify_success.style.display = "none";
                
                var verify_fail = document.getElementById("verify_fail");
                verify_fail.style.display = "block";*/	
                 
            }
          }
        });
        
    }

 <!--js for timer-->    
<script>
      function timer(duration) {
        var timerModal = document.getElementById("timeout");
        var timerElement = document.getElementById("timer");
        var minutes, seconds;
    
        console.log(`Timer for ${duration} seconds started!`);
        timerModal.style.display = "block";
        document.getElementsByClassName("close")[0].onclick = function() {
          timerModal.style.display = "none";
        };
    
        var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
          minutes = parseInt(duration / 60, 10);
          seconds = parseInt(duration % 60, 10);
    
          minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
          seconds = seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;
    
          timerElement.innerHTML = minutes + ":" + seconds;
    
          if (--duration < 0) {
            clearInterval(intervalId);
            timerElement.innerHTML = "Time's up!";
            setTimeout(function(){
              location.reload();
            }, 2000); 
          }
        }, 1000);    
      }
      
    </script>
<!--js for time ends-->

<script>
function open_i_frame_front() {
  var ord_id = document.getElementById('ORDER_ID').value ;
  var cust = document.getElementById('CUST_ID').value ;
  var ind = document.getElementById('INDUSTRY_TYPE_ID').value ;
  var chan = document.getElementById('CHANNEL_ID').value ;
  var amt = document.getElementById('TXN_AMOUNT').value ;

  
  var dataString = '&ORDER_ID='+ord_id+'&CUST_ID='+cust+'&INDUSTRY_TYPE_ID='+ind+'&CHANNEL_ID='+chan+'&TXN_AMOUNT='+amt ;   

      // alert(dataString);
      $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Paytm/pgRedirect_ajax',
          data:dataString,        
          success: function (response) {
              // var data = JSON.parse(response);
              // var status = data.status;
              // alert('ok');
              $("#form_iframe").html(response);
              document.getElementById("form_buy_coupon").style.display = "none";
              document.getElementById("form_iframe").style.display = "";
            //   $('#createDistributor').modal('show');
                        
  
              }        
          
      });

}
</script>

function save_form_paytm(paytype) {
  
//   var user_no = document.getElementById('user_no').value ;

    var ord_id = document.getElementById("ORDER_ID").value;

    var damt = Number(amt).toFixed(2) ;   
    
    // var pay_type = 'paytm' ;
    var pay_type = paytype ;
    var u_id = document.getElementById("CUST_ID").value  ;

    var admin_pk = '';

  var dataString = '&u_id='+u_id+'&admin_id='+admin_pk+'&pay_type='+pay_type+'&ord_id='+ord_id+'&TXN_AMOUNT='+damt;
      //alert(dataString);

          type: 'POST',
          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/add_transection',

              console.log(response);

              var status = data.status;
              if(status == 'success'){
                // alert('Saved ');

                if( pay_type=='hdfc'){
                  //alert('ok');

                open_i_frame_front();
                }

                    }
                    else{
                      alert('Something went Wrong Please try again ');
                      location.reload();
                    }              
  
              }        
          
      });
          }
      
      </script>

<script>
    
    function couponData()
    {
        //alert("sachin");
        
        var pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("pay_type_coupon").value;
        var upiid_coupon = document.getElementById("upiid_coupon").value;
        var checkboxValue = document.getElementById("term_c").checked;
        
            if (pay_type_coupon == '') 
            { 
            alert('SELECT PAYMENT TYPE.');
            }
            else if (upiid_coupon == '') 
            {
            alert('Enter UPI ID');
            }
            else if (checkboxValue === false)
            {
            alert('Select terms and conditions');
            } 
            else
            {
                saverecordfirst();
                var couponButton = document.getElementById("pay_coupon");
                // couponButton.parentNode.removeChild(couponButton);
            }
              
    }
    
</script>


<script>
    
   function saverecordfirst()
    {
        //alert("saverecordfirst");
        var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        
        var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon").value;
        
        var total_cou_amt = parseFloat(document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent);

        var user_amt = parseFloat(document.getElementById("shows_amount").textContent);
        
        var order_id_coup = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value;
        
        var user_id_val = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
        
        var mobile = document.getElementById("coup_mob").value;
        var rem_c = document.getElementById("rem_c").value;
        
        var no_of_coupon = document.getElementById("no_of_coupon").textContent;
        
        
        
       /* alert(hdfc_pay_c_type);
        
        alert(hdfc_pay_type_coupon);
        
        alert(total_cou_amt);
        
        alert(order_id_coup);
        
        alert(user_id_val);
        alert(mobile);
        
        alert(no_of_coupon);*/
        
        
        
            $.ajax({
    			url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/save_coupon_homepage',
    			type: 'POST',
    			data: { 
    				user_id:user_id_val,
    				order_id: order_id_coup,
    				amount:total_cou_amt,
            user_amt:user_amt,
            wl_id:'',
    				pay_type:hdfc_pay_type_coupon,
    				coupon_type:hdfc_pay_c_type,
    				mobile:mobile,
            rem_c:rem_c,
    				no_coupon:no_of_coupon
    			},
    			success: function(response) {
    				var data = JSON.parse(response);
    				if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
    				    //alert('save');
    				    savecoupon_Data();
    				    
    				   	}
    				else{
    					//alert('not saved');
    				}
    			}
    		}); 
        
        
    }
    
</script>








<script>
    function savecoupon_Data()
    {  
        //alert("sachin");
       
        var pg_id_coupon = document.getElementById("pg_id_coupon");
        var upiid_coupon = document.getElementById("upiid_coupon");
        var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon");
        var total_cou_amt = parseInt(document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent);
        var order_id_coup = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value ;
        
        var user_id_val = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
        
        var payer_name_coupon = upiid_coupon.value;
        var pgmerid_coupon = pg_id_coupon.value;
        var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = hdfc_pay_type_coupon.value;
        
         var checkboxValue = document.getElementById("term_c").checked; 
         
         var rem = document.getElementById("rem_c").value;
         
         //alert(total_cou_amt);
         
          //var transcou_amt =1;
         
         
        
            if (total_cou_amt>0 && checkboxValue == true) {
               //alert("trans save");
                     $.ajax({
                        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/hdfc_trans_amount_save',
                        type: 'POST',
                        data: { 
                        amount: total_cou_amt, 
                        payer_name: payer_name_coupon,
                        pgmerid:pgmerid_coupon,
                        order_no:order_id_coup,
                        id:user_id_val,
                        rem:rem
                        },
                        success: function(response) {
                        var data = JSON.parse(response);
                        var msg=data.msg;
                       if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                           //alert("sachin");
                           successcoupData();
                        }
                        else{
                           var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('t_failed_c'), {
                                    keyboard: false,
		                            backdrop: 'static' 
                            });
                            paymentModal.show();
                             var tc_failed = document.getElementById("tc_failed_c"); 
                           tc_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                              location.reload();
                            });
                            
                        }
                      }
                    });
                
                
            }
        //    
     }  
     
</script>






<script>
 function successcoupData()
    {
       // alert("sachin");
        var payer_name = document.getElementById("upiid_coupon").value;
        
        var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        
        var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon").value;;
        
        var total_cou_amt = document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent;
        
        var order_id = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value ;
        
        var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
        
         var no_of_coupon = document.getElementById("no_of_coupon").textContent;
        
        var pgmerid = 'HDFC000022529749';
        
        /*alert(payer_name);
        alert(hdfc_pay_c_type);//coupon type
        alert(hdfc_pay_type_coupon);//pay type==hdfc
        alert(total_cou_amt);
        
         alert(order_id);
         
         alert(user_id);*/
         
         console.log('total_cou_amt');
        
        
                $.ajax({
                url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/hdfc_trans_collect_prod',
                type: 'POST',
                data: { 
                payer_name: payer_name,
                pgmerid:pgmerid,
                amount:total_cou_amt,
                order_no:order_id,
                id:user_id
                },
                success: function(response) {
                console.log(response); 
                //exit();
                var data = JSON.parse(response);
                var msg=data.msg;
                var upi=data.upi;
                var orderno=data.orderno;
                var amt=data.amt;
                var vpaid=data.vpaid;
                var pg_id='HDFC000022529749';
               if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                   timerc(300);//test
                    // Define a variable to store the interval
                    var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
                        $.ajax({
                            url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/hdfc_trans_status_prod',
                            type: 'POST',
                            data: { 
                                pg_id:pg_id,
                                orderno: orderno,
                                upi:upi,
                                user_id:user_id
                            },
                            success: function(response) {
                                console.log(response);
                                var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                var cust_ref_no=data.cust_ref_no;
                                var vpaid=data.vpaid;
                                var amt=data.amt;
                                var status=data.status;
                                if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
                                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval
                                    var timeout_close = document.getElementById("timeout_c"); 
                                    timeout_close.style.display = "none";
                                    var customer_Receipt = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('customer_Receipt_c'), {
                                        keyboard: false,
		                                backdrop: 'static' 
                                    });
                                    document.getElementById("msg_c").innerHTML = status;
                                    document.getElementById("upi_txn_no_c").innerHTML = upi;
                                    document.getElementById("order_no_c").innerHTML = orderno; 
                                    document.getElementById("tt_amt_c").innerHTML = amt;
                                    document.getElementById("cust_ref_no_c").innerHTML = cust_ref_no;
                                    document.getElementById("vppaid_c").innerHTML = vpaid;
                                    customer_Receipt.show();
                                    
                                    var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        
                            		var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon").value;
                            		
                            		var order_id_coup = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value ;
                            		
                            		var no_of_coupon = document.getElementById("no_of_coupon").textContent;
                            		  
                            		var total_cou_amt = parseInt(document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent);
                            		
                            		var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
                            		
                            		var server = 'bitspanindia.com';
		
		                            var dataString = '&user_no=' + no_of_coupon + '&server=' + server +'&user_pk=' + user_id + '&upi=' + upi + '&coupon_type=' + hdfc_pay_c_type + '&pay_type=' + hdfc_pay_type_coupon + '&ord_id=' + order_id_coup + '&TXN_AMOUNT=' + total_cou_amt + '&status=' + status;
                                      
                                     $.ajax({
                                          type: 'POST',
                                          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/save_buy_coupon',
                                          data:dataString,        
                                          success: function (response) {
                                              var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                              var status = data.status;
                                              if(status == 'SUCCESS'){
                                                    console.log('updated');
                                                    }
                                                    else{
                                                      alert('Something went Wrong Please try again ');
                                                      location.reload();
                                                    }              
                                  
                                              }        
                                          
                                      });
                                    
                                    //
                                    var close_receipt = document.getElementById("close_receipt_c"); 
                                    close_receipt.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                        location.reload();
                                        
                                    });
                                    
                                    
                                }
                                else if (data.status === 'REJECTED') {
                                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval
                                    var timeout_close = document.getElementById("timeout_c"); 
                                    timeout_close.style.display = "none";
                                    var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('trnas_failed_c'), {
                                        keyboard: false,
		                                backdrop: 'static' 
                                    });
                                    document.getElementById("fail_msg_c").innerHTML = status; 
                                    document.getElementById("f_amt_c").innerHTML = amt; 
                                    document.getElementById("f_upi_c").innerHTML = upi;
                                    document.getElementById("f_order_no_c").innerHTML = orderno; 
                                    document.getElementById("f_cust_ref_no_c").innerHTML = cust_ref_no;
                                    document.getElementById("vpaid_c").innerHTML = vpaid; 
                                    paymentModal.show();
                                    
                                    var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        
                            		var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon").value;
                            		
                            		var order_id_coup = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value ;
                            		
                            		var no_of_coupon = document.getElementById("no_of_coupon").textContent;
                            		
                            		var total_cou_amt = parseInt(document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent);
                            		  
                            		 var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
		
		                            var server = 'bitspanindia.com';
		
		                            var dataString = '&user_no=' + no_of_coupon + '&server=' + server +'&user_pk=' + user_id + '&upi=' + upi + '&coupon_type=' + hdfc_pay_c_type + '&pay_type=' + hdfc_pay_type_coupon + '&ord_id=' + order_id_coup + '&TXN_AMOUNT=' + total_cou_amt + '&status=' + status;
                                                                        
                                     $.ajax({
                                          type: 'POST',
                                          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/save_buy_coupon',
                                          data:dataString,        
                                          success: function (response) {
                                              var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                              var status = data.status;
                                              if(status == 'SUCCESS'){
                                                 console.log('updated');
                                                    }
                                                    else{
                                                      alert('Something went Wrong Please try again ');
                                                      location.reload();
                                                    }              
                                  
                                              }        
                                          
                                      });
                                        
                                    //
                                    var close_failed = document.getElementById("close_failed_c"); 
                                    close_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                         location.reload();
                                       
                                    });
                                }
                                //
                                else if (data.status === 'FAILED') {
                                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop the interval
                                    var timeout_close = document.getElementById("timeout_c"); 
                                    timeout_close.style.display = "none";
                                    var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('trnas_failed_c'), {
                                        keyboard: false,
		                                backdrop: 'static' 
                                    });
                                    document.getElementById("fail_msg_c").innerHTML = status; 
                                    document.getElementById("f_amt_c").innerHTML = amt; 
                                    document.getElementById("f_upi_c").innerHTML = upi;
                                    document.getElementById("f_order_no_c").innerHTML = orderno; 
                                    document.getElementById("f_cust_ref_no_c").innerHTML = cust_ref_no;
                                    document.getElementById("vpaid_c").innerHTML = vpaid; 
                                    paymentModal.show();
                                    var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        
                            		var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon").value;
                            		
                            		var order_id_coup = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value ;
                            		
                            		var no_of_coupon = document.getElementById("no_of_coupon").textContent;
                            		
                            		var total_cou_amt = parseInt(document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent);
                            		  
                            		 var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
		
		                            var server = 'bitspanindia.com';
		
		                            var dataString = '&user_no=' + no_of_coupon + '&server=' + server +'&user_pk=' + user_id + '&upi=' + upi + '&coupon_type=' + hdfc_pay_c_type + '&pay_type=' + hdfc_pay_type_coupon + '&ord_id=' + order_id_coup + '&TXN_AMOUNT=' + total_cou_amt + '&status=' + status;
                                                                        
                                     $.ajax({
                                          type: 'POST',
                                          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/save_buy_coupon',
                                          data:dataString,        
                                          success: function (response) {
                                              var data = JSON.parse(response);
                                              var status = data.status;
                                              if(status == 'SUCCESS'){
                                                  console.log('updated');
                                                // alert('Saved ');
                                                // document.getElementById("btn_paytm").click();
                                                //open_i_frame();
                                                    }
                                                    else{
                                                      alert('Something went Wrong Please try again ');
                                                      location.reload();
                                                    }              
                                  
                                              }        
                                          
                                      });
                                        
                                    //
                                    var close_failed = document.getElementById("close_failed_c"); 
                                    close_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                                         location.reload();
                                       
                                    });
                                }  
                                
                                
                            //    
                            }
                        });
                    }, 2000);
                   
                   
             //  
            }
            else{
               var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('trnas_collect_failed_c'), {
                        keyboard: false,
		                backdrop: 'static' 
                });
                document.getElementById("fail_msg_c").innerHTML = status; 
                document.getElementById("vpaid_c").innerHTML = vpaid; 
                paymentModal.show();
                var close_failed = document.getElementById("trans_close_failed_c"); 
               close_failed.addEventListener("click", function() {
                  location.reload();
                });
                
                
            }
          }
        });
        
    }
    
</script>

<!--js for timer-->
<script>
      function timerc(duration) {
        var timerModal = document.getElementById("timeout_c");
        var timerElement = document.getElementById("timer_p");
        var minutes, seconds;
    
        console.log(`Timer for ${duration} seconds started!`);
    
        // Display the modal when the timer function is called
        timerModal.style.display = "block";
    
        // When the user clicks on the close button, hide the modal
        document.getElementsByClassName("close")[0].onclick = function() {
          timerModal.style.display = "none";
        };
    
        var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
          minutes = parseInt(duration / 60, 10);
          seconds = parseInt(duration % 60, 10);
    
          minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
          seconds = seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;
    
          timerElement.innerHTML = minutes + ":" + seconds;
    
          if (--duration < 0) {
            clearInterval(intervalId);
            timerElement.innerHTML = "Time's up!";
            setTimeout(function(){
              location.reload();
            }, 2000); // Reload the page after 2 seconds (2000 milliseconds)
          }
        }, 1000);    
      }
      
    </script>
<!--js for time ends-->

<script>
    $("#pay_type_coupon").change(function() {
          var value = $(this).val(); 
          //alert(value); 
          if(value=='hdfc')
          {
           var element = document.getElementById("hdfc_sub_coupon");
            element.style.display = "block";
            
            
            var shows_amount = document.getElementById("shows_amount").textContent;
            //console.log(shows_amount);
            
            var conv_charge_coupon = '0';
            
            var payout_hdfc_type = 'fixed';
            
            
            console.log(payout_hdfc_type);
            
                if(payout_hdfc_type=='percentage') 
                {
                
                    //console.log(conv_charge_coupon);
                    
                    var conv_charge_coupon=conv_charge_coupon/100;;
                    
                    var coupon_sum=0;
                    
                    coupon_sum = parseInt(shows_amount) * conv_charge_coupon;
                    
                    coupon_sum = coupon_sum + parseInt(shows_amount) 
                    
                    //console.log(coupon_sum);
                    
                    document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").innerHTML = coupon_sum;
                }
                else
                {
                    var coupon_sum=0;
                    
                    coupon_sum = parseInt(shows_amount) +parseInt(conv_charge_coupon);
                    
                    //console.log(coupon_sum);
                    
                    document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").innerHTML = coupon_sum;
                }
                    
             
             
          }
          if(value=='NULL')
          {
            var element = document.getElementById("hdfc_sub_coupon");
            element.style.display = "none";
            
          }
          
        });
    
</script>


<script>
    function verifycouponVpa(val){
        //alert("verifyvpa");
        var a11 = document.getElementById("a12");
        var pay_coupon = document.getElementById("pay_coupon");
        
        var upiid = document.getElementById("upiid").value;
        var vpaid=val;
        var pg_id = document.getElementById("pg_id");
        
        var user_id = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;  
       
        
        var pg_id='HDFC000022529749';
        
        //alert(user_id);
        
        var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/verify_vpaid';
        /*alert(ac);
        */
        $.ajax({
          url: ac,
          type: 'POST',
          data: { 
            vpaid: vpaid,
            pg_id:pg_id,
            user_id:user_id
          },
          success: function(response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            if (data.status === 'VE') {
                a12.style.display = "block";
                //document.getElementById("a11").innerHTML = "Verified";
               document.getElementById("a12").innerHTML='<img src="https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/assest/img/success.gif" style="width: 3rem; height: 3rem;" >';
                pay_coupon.disabled = false;
                document.getElementById("pay_coupon").disabled = false;
                
            }
            else{
                 a12.style.display = "block";
                 
                //document.getElementById("a11").innerHTML = "Not Verified";
                document.getElementById("a12").innerHTML = '<img src="https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/assest/img/failed.gif" style="width: 2rem; height: 2rem;">';
                pay_coupon.disabled = true;
                document.getElementById("pay_coupon").disabled = true;
               
               
                 
            }
          }
        });
        
    }
    
    
   </script>

<script>
function open_i_frame() {
  var ord_id = document.getElementById('ORDER_ID').value ;
  var cust = document.getElementById('CUST_ID').value ;
  var ind = document.getElementById('INDUSTRY_TYPE_ID').value ;
  var chan = document.getElementById('CHANNEL_ID').value ;
  var amt = document.getElementById('TXN_AMOUNT').value ;

  
  var dataString = '&ORDER_ID='+ord_id+'&CUST_ID='+cust+'&INDUSTRY_TYPE_ID='+ind+'&CHANNEL_ID='+chan+'&TXN_AMOUNT='+amt ;   

      alert(dataString); exit;
      $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Paytm/pgRedirect_ajax',
          data:dataString,        
          success: function (response) {
              // var data = JSON.parse(response);
              // var status = data.status;
              $("#form_iframe").html(response);
              document.getElementById("form_buy_coupon").style.display = "none";
              document.getElementById("form_iframe").style.display = "";
              
                        
  
              }        
          
      });

}
</script>

    

<script>
function save_form() {
  
//   var user_no = document.getElementById('user_no').value ;
//   var pay_type = document.getElementById('pay_type').value ;

//   var coupon_type = document.getElementById('pay_c_type').value ;
//   var ord_id = document.getElementById('ORDER_ID').value ;
  
//   var amt = document.getElementById('TXN_AMOUNT').value ;

//   var dataString = '&user_no='+user_no+'&coupon_type='+coupon_type+'&pay_type='+pay_type+'&ord_id='+ord_id+'&TXN_AMOUNT='+damt ;
    var dataString = $('#user_form').serialize() ;
      alert(dataString);
      $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/ajax_save_user',
          data:dataString,        
          success: function (response) {
              var data = JSON.parse(response);
              var status = data.status;
              if(status == 'success'){
                // alert('Saved ');
                // document.getElementById("btn_paytm").click();
                open_i_frame();
                    }
                    else{
                      alert('Something went Wrong Please try again ');
                      location.reload();
                    }              
  
              }        
          
      });
          }
      
      </script>

                      placeholder="" onkeyup="id_detail(this.value)">
                      <label for="floatingInput">Enter Phone Number</label>
                    </div>
                </form>
                <div class="text-center" id="id_detail">
                    <!-- <span class="badge bg-light text-dark">mohit@gmail.com</span><br>
                    <span class="badge bg-light text-dark">abc@gmail.com</span><br>
                    <span class="badge bg-light text-dark">xyz@gmail.com</span> -->
                    <script>
                      function id_detail(val){

  var dataString = '&u_id='+val;
       
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/get_user_details',
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var html_content = data.html_content;
            // console.log(data.u_data);
            $('#id_detail').html('');
            
            if(html_content != ''){
              $('#id_detail').html(html_content);

                  }
                  else{
                $('#id_detail').html('');
                  }           

                        }        
        
    });
        }
                      </script>
                </div>
            </div>
          </div>
    
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

<script>
function myFunction()
{
     var user_id_val = document.getElementById("user_id_ver").value;
     var copType = document.getElementById("copType").value;
     var cop_value = document.getElementById("cop_value").value;
     var coup_mob = document.getElementById("coup_mob").value;
     
     if(user_id_val=='')
     {
         alert("Enter USER ID");
     }
     else if(copType=='')
     {
         alert("Enter Coupon type");
     }
     else if(cop_value=='')
     {
         alert("Enter No of Coupon");
     }
     else if(coup_mob=='')
     {
         alert("Enter Mobile No");
     }
     else
     { 
         var paymentModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('couponModal'), {
            keyboard: false,
            backdrop: 'static' 
            });
            paymentModal.show();
            document.getElementById('couponModal')
             var buyCouponbutton = document.getElementById("buyCoupon");
             buyCouponbutton.style.display = "none";  
    }
}
</script>

    <script>
    
    
    
    
    
      function formatEmail(email, hiddenCharactersCount) {
                var parts = email.split('@');
                var username = parts[0];
                var domain = parts[1];

                var hiddenPart = '*'.repeat(hiddenCharactersCount);

                var formattedEmail = username.slice(0, -hiddenCharactersCount) + hiddenPart + '@' + domain;
                return formattedEmail;
            }
            
       
             function send_sms_11() {
            
            var u_ide = document.getElementById("user_id_e_forget_pass").value;
            var send_type = document.getElementById("send_type").value;
            
           
            document.getElementById("otp-btn").style.display = "none";
         
              $.ajax({
            url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/cross_Verified/'+ u_ide + '/' + send_type ,
            type: 'POST',
            data:  '', 
            success: function(response) {
            
            
             var data = JSON.parse(response);
            console.log(data);
             if(data.status=='success'){
                 
                 
                 
                 var email = data.email;
                 var redirectURL = data.url;
                 
                  var formattedEmail = formatEmail(email, 4);
                  
                 
                 alert("Reset Password link has been send to your email " + formattedEmail);
                 
                  $.ajax({
            url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Demo/send_mail_link/'+ u_ide + '/' + email+ '/' + send_type  ,
            type: 'POST',
            data:  '', 
            success: function(response) {
              var data = JSON.parse(response);
            
             console.log(data);
             if(data.status == 2){
              document.getElementById("otp-btn").style.display = "";
             }else{
                 window.location.href = redirectURL;
             }
            
               
            }
        });
                 
                 
                 
                 
                 
                 
                 
                 
                //  
                 
             }else{
              document.getElementById("otp-btn").style.display = "";
                  $('#err_msge').html("Entered Email/Phone Number doesn't Match With your account .Please Enter valid Details .");
                     u_ide.val('');
                 send_type.val('') ;
             }
            
               
            }
        });
            
            
        }
       
    </script>

<script>
    function change_pass_new(){
        
                var password = document.getElementById("new_pass").value;
        var confirmPassword = document.getElementById("confirm_pass").value;
        if (password != confirmPassword) {
            alert("Passwords do not match. Please Confirm Password ");
           exit;
        }else{
           var u_ide = document.getElementById("user_id_e_forget_pass").value;
           
            var dataString = '&password='+password+'&user_id='+u_ide ;
    // alert(dataString) ;
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/change_pass_new',
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var status = data.status;
            if(status == 'success'){
             
              $('#otp_msg_3').html("Password changed Successfully .");
              alert('Password changed Successfully .') ;
              location.reload();
                  }
                  else{
                        $('#otp_msg_3').html("Something went wrong ."); 
                  }
						}        
        
    });
        }
        
    }
    function Validate_pass() {
        var password = document.getElementById("new_pass").value;
        var confirmPassword = document.getElementById("confirm_pass").value;
        if (password != confirmPassword) {
            alert("Passwords do not match. Please Confirm Password ");
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }
</script>

    <script>
        $(document).ready(function(e){
            
 var timeout;
        var delay = 1000;
  $('[data-id="user_ide"]').keyup(function(e) {
      
      document.getElementById("cop_value").value = '';

document.getElementById("copType").value = '';
// document.getElementById("total_amt")innerHTML = '';;

      var user_id_c = document.getElementById("user_id_ver").value;
      
       user_id_val.innerHTML = user_id_c;
           
            var va = this.value ;
        //   console.log(va);
            // var name = $(this).attr('id');
            var id = this.getAttribute('id');
            // console.log(id);
            
           
             
            if(timeout) {
                clearTimeout(timeout);
            }
            timeout = setTimeout(function() {              
                myFun(va , id);
            }, delay);
        });
        
        
       function myFun(user_id , id) {
    //  console.log(user_id ,id);
var dataString = '&u_id='+user_id ;
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Admin/verify_userId',
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var status = data.status;
            if(status == 'success'){
              if(id =='user_id_ver'){
                // console.log(data);
                $('#st_suc1').html(""); 
                $('#st_dan2').html(""); 
                
                $('#st_suc1').html("User ID is correct "); 
document.getElementById('user_type_coupon_buy').value = '';

document.getElementById('user_type_coupon_buy').value = data.u_type;

document.getElementById("cop_value").value = '';

document.getElementById("copType").value = '';


                $('#btn_send_wl').show();
              }
                  }
                  else{
                    if(id == 'user_id_ver'){
                      $('#st_dan2').html(""); 
                      $('#st_suc1').html("");
                    $('#st_dan2').html("You entered the wrong id"); 
                     $('#btn_send_wl').hide();
                    }
                  }
            

						}        
        
    });
        } 
        
        
        
         // for testing  
         $('[data-id="user_idtest"]').keyup(function(e) {
      
      
           
            var va = this.value ;
        //   console.log(va);

        });
        
        
       function myTes(user_id , id) {
    //  console.log(user_id ,id);
var dataString = '&u_id='+user_id ;
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Admin/verify_userId',
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var status = data.status;
            // console.log(data);
            if(status == 'success'){
              if(id =='user_id_vertd'){
                $('#tes_ted2').html(""); 
                
                $('#tes_ted').html("User ID is correct "); 

             $('#user_roledb').val(data.u_type) ;
             $('#user_prkey').val(data.u_data[0].id) ;


                $('#tested_btn').show();
              }
                  }
                  else{
                    if(id == 'user_id_vertd'){
                       
                      $('#tes_ted').html("");
                    $('#tes_ted2').html("You entered the wrong id"); 
                     $('#tested_btn').hide();
                    }
                  }
            

						}        
        
    });
        }  
        
        
        
        
        
          $('[data-id="user_idwl"]').click(function() {
      
 var va = this.value ;
     
           
            var id = this.getAttribute('id');
    //   console.log(va);
            if(timeout) {
                clearTimeout(timeout);
            }
            timeout = setTimeout(function() {              
                myVerify(va , id);
            }, delay);
        });
        
          function myVerify(user_id , id) {
    //  console.log(user_id ,id);
var dataString = '&u_id='+user_id ;

    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Admin/check_userId',
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var status = data.status;
            if(status == 'success'){
              if(id =='user_idwl'){
                // console.log(data);
                $('#us_phone').val(data.u_data[0].phone) ;
                 $('#srcre').val(data.u_data[0].phone) ;
                $('#err_msge').html(""); 
                
                $('#ss_msge').html("User ID is correct "); 



                $('#sub-btn').show();
              }
                  }
                  else{
                    if(id == 'user_idwl'){
                     
                      $('#ss_msge').html("");
                    $('#err_msge').html("You entered the wrong id"); 
                     $('#sub-btn').hide();
                    }
                  }
            

						}        
        
    });
        }

  function showPrice(){
    //  var e_price = 101;
    //  var p_price = 73;
   var u_type =  document.getElementById('user_type_coupon_buy').value ;
    if(u_type == 'RETAILER'){
       var p_price = '100';
     var e_price = '70';
    }
    else if(u_type == 'DISTRIBUTOR'){
       var p_price = '98';
     var e_price = '68';
    }
    else if(u_type == 'SUPER DISTRIBUTOR'){
       var p_price = '97';
     var e_price = '67';
    }
    else if(u_type == 'WHITE LABEL'){
       var p_price = '97';
     var e_price = '68';
    }
    else if(u_type == 'UTI PSA ID'){
       var p_price = '101';
     var e_price = '73';
    }

     var getNum = document.getElementById("cop_value");
     var check = getNum.value;
     no_of_coupon.innerHTML = check;
     var c_type = document.getElementById("copType");
var typCoupon = c_type.options[c_type.selectedIndex].text;
type_coupon.innerHTML = typCoupon;
   
     var showTotal = document.getElementById("total_amt");
     if(typCoupon =="P-Coupon"){
         var result = p_price * check ; 
     }else{
         var result = e_price * check ; 
     }
  showTotal.innerHTML = result;
  shows_amount.innerHTML = result;
  }
 function showRole(){
    
     role_type.innerHTML = 'retailer';
 }

    <script>
                              function submit_form_join(id , btn_submit){
                                var dataString = $("#"+id).serialize() ;

                                var pay = document.getElementById("pay");
        pay.disabled = false;

                                // console.log(dataString);
                                // new_distributor_ajax

                                // var dataString = '&u_id='+val;
        
        if(id == 'save_distributor'){
        var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/new_distributor_ajax'
        }else if(id == 'save_retailor'){
        var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/new_retailor_ajax'
        }
        else if(id == 'save_super_distributor'){
          var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/addNewSuper_ajax'
        }
        else if(id == 'save_super_distributor'){
          var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/addWhite_label_ajax'
        }

        //alert(ac);   
        // exit();
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: ac,
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var html_content = data.html_content;
            // console.log(data);
           if(data.status=='success'){
            document.getElementById("order_id").value = data.order_id;
            document.getElementById("user_id").value = data.ud;
            document.getElementById(btn_submit).click();
            var pay = document.getElementById("pay");
        pay.disabled = false;

        document.getElementById('btn_'+id).click();
           }else{
            var msg = data.msg;
            alert(msg);
           }

                        }        
        
    });
                              }
                              </script>

function replaceAllText() {
    // console.log('chng');
  replaceText('*', 'BITS', 'bitspanindia.com', 'g');
   replaceText('*', 'logo.jpg', '', 'g');
}

// $(document).ready(replaceAllText);
// $('html').ajaxStop(replaceAllText);


function replaceText(selector, text, newText, flags) {
  var matcher = new RegExp(text, flags);
  $(selector).each(function () {
    var $this = $(this);
    if (!$this.children().length)
      $this.text($this.text().replace(matcher, newText));
  });
}

  <script>
                              function submit_form_join_new(id , btn_submit){

                                var checkboxValue = document.getElementById("term_"+id).checked;

                                if(checkboxValue=='')
              {
                   alert('Select term and condition');
                   exit();
              }                     
              
                                // document.getElementById("pay_btn_"+id).remove() ;
                                var dataString = $("#"+id).serialize() ;

                                // var pay = document.getElementById("pay");
                                //     pay.disabled = false;

                                // console.log(dataString);
                                // new_distributor_ajax

                                // var dataString = '&u_id='+val;
        
        if(id == 'save_distributor'){
        var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/new_distributor_ajax' ;
        var trans_amt = document.getElementById("joining_distributor").value;
        
        }else if(id == 'save_retailor'){
        var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/new_retailor_ajax' ;
        var trans_amt = document.getElementById("joining_retailor").value;
        
        }
        else if(id == 'save_super_distributor'){
          var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/addNewSuper_ajax' ;
          var trans_amt = document.getElementById("joining_superdist").value;
        }
        else if(id == 'save_super_distributor'){
          var ac = 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/addWhite_label_ajax'
        }

        //alert(ac);   
        // exit();

       

    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: ac,
        data:dataString,        
        success: function (response) {
            var data = JSON.parse(response);
            var html_content = data.html_content;
            // console.log(data);
           if(data.status=='success'){
            // document.getElementById("order_id").value = data.order_id;
            // document.getElementById("user_id").value = data.ud;

            // var joiningDistributorValue = document.getElementById("joining_distributor").value;

                        
            var conv_charge = '0';
            
            var payout_hdfc_type = 'fixed';
            
            
                if(payout_hdfc_type=='percentage')
                {
                conv_charge = conv_charge/100;
                
                var sum = 0;
                
                sum = parseFloat(trans_amt) * conv_charge;
                
                var conv11 = sum ; 
                //console.log(sum);
                
                sum = sum + parseFloat(trans_amt);
                
                //console.log(sum);
                
                // document.getElementById("amount_charge_text").innerHTML = sum;
                
                var txn=0;
                txn=sum;
                
                //console.log(txn);
                // alert(txn); 
                // document.getElementById("TXN_AMOUNT").value = txn;
                $('#TXN_AMOUNT_HDFC').val(txn);
                }
                else
                {
                    var sum = 0;
                    sum = parseFloat(trans_amt) +parseFloat(conv_charge);
                    
                    var conv11 = conv_charge ;

                    //console.log(sum);
                    
                    // document.getElementById("amount_charge_text").innerHTML = sum;
                    
                    var txn=0;
                    txn=sum;
                    
                    //console.log(txn);
                    // alert(txn);
                    
                    // document.getElementById("TXN_AMOUNT").value = txn;
                    $('#TXN_AMOUNT_HDFC').val(txn);
                }
                
                $('#ORDER_ID_HDFC').val(data.order_id);
                $('#MID_HDFC').val(data.ud);
                $('#CUST_ID_HDFC').val(data.ud);

                $('#CONV_CHARGE_HDFC').val(conv11);
                $('#MAIN_AMOUNT_HDFC').val(trans_amt);

                    var full_call = 'index.php/Homepage/pay24Response'
                $('#WEB_CALLBACK_URL_HDFC').val('https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/'+full_call);
     
        document.getElementById("pay_btn_"+id).remove() ;

        save_form_hdfc_new();
        
           }else{
            var msg = data.msg;
            alert(msg);
           }

                        }        
        
    });
                              }
                              </script>




<script>
function save_form_hdfc_new() {
  
    var pay_type = 'hdfc' ;

    var ord_id = document.getElementById("ORDER_ID_HDFC").value;    

  var amt = document.getElementById('MAIN_AMOUNT_HDFC').value ;
  
    var damt = Number(amt).toFixed(2) ;   
    
    // var pay_type = 'paytm' ;
    
    var ref_code =  document.getElementById('ref_code_main').value ;;
   
    var u_id = document.getElementById("CUST_ID_HDFC").value  ;

    var admin_pk = '';

  var dataString = '&u_id='+u_id+'&admin_id='+admin_pk+'&pay_type='+pay_type+'&ord_id='+ord_id+'&TXN_AMOUNT='+damt+'&ref_code='+ref_code;
    //   alert(dataString);
      //exit();
      $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/add_transection',
          data:dataString,        
          success: function (response) {
            //   console.log(response);
              var data = JSON.parse(response);
              var status = data.status;
            //   console.log(data);
              if(status == 'success'){
                // alert('Saved ');
                // document.getElementById("btn_paytm").click();
                if( pay_type=='hdfc'){                 
                    var final_pay_amount = data.final_pay_amount;
                    
                    document.getElementById('MAIN_AMOUNT_HDFC').value = final_pay_amount ;
                    
                     document.getElementById('TXN_AMOUNT_HDFC').value = final_pay_amount ;
                    
                document.getElementById('btn_pay_hdfc').click();

                }else{
                open_i_frame_front();
                }

                    }
                    else{
                      alert('Something went Wrong Please try again ......');
                    //   location.reload();
                    }              
  
              }        
          
      });
          }
      
      </script>
