<script>

function saverecordfirst_new()
    {
        // alert("saverecordfirst");


        var conv_charge = '0';
            
            var payout_hdfc_type = 'fixed';
            
            var user_amt = parseFloat(document.getElementById("shows_amount").textContent); 

            var trans_amt = user_amt ;
            
                if(payout_hdfc_type=='percentage')
                {
                conv_charge = conv_charge/100;
                
                var sum = 0;
                
                sum = parseFloat(trans_amt) * conv_charge;
                
                var conv11 = sum ; 
                //console.log(sum);
                
                sum = sum + parseFloat(trans_amt);
                                
                var txn=0;
                txn=sum;
                
                $('#TXN_AMOUNT_HDFC').val(txn);
                }
                else
                {
                    var sum = 0;
                    sum = parseFloat(trans_amt) +parseFloat(conv_charge);
                    
                    var conv11 = conv_charge ;

                    
                    var txn=0;
                    txn=sum;
                    
                    $('#TXN_AMOUNT_HDFC').val(txn);
                }
              
                // var total_cou_amt = parseFloat(document.getElementById("amount_charge_coupon").textContent);

                var total_cou_amt = parseFloat(txn);
                                
        var hdfc_pay_c_type = document.getElementById("type_coupon").textContent;
        
        var hdfc_pay_type_coupon = document.getElementById("hdfc_pay_type_coupon").value;
              
        
        // var order_id_coup = document.getElementById('order_id_coup').value;
        
        var order_id_coup = 'BUY_COUPON4728674847316' ;
        
        var user_id_val = document.getElementById("user_id_val").textContent;
        
        var mobile = document.getElementById("coup_mob").value;
        var rem_c = document.getElementById("rem_c").value;
        
        var no_of_coupon = document.getElementById("no_of_coupon").textContent;

        $.ajax({
    			url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/homepage/save_coupon_homepage',
    			type: 'POST',
    			data: { 
    				user_id:user_id_val,
    				order_id: order_id_coup,
    				amount:total_cou_amt,
                    user_amt:user_amt,
                    wl_id:'',
    				pay_type:hdfc_pay_type_coupon,
    				coupon_type:hdfc_pay_c_type,
    				mobile:mobile,
                    rem_c:rem_c,
    				no_coupon:no_of_coupon
    			},
    			success: function(response) {
    				var data = JSON.parse(response);
    				if (data.status === 'SUCCESS') {
    				    //alert('save');
    				    // savecoupon_Data();

                        // $('#ORDER_ID_HDFC').val(order_id_coup);
                        //  $response['order_id11'] = $ord_id ;
                $('#ORDER_ID_HDFC').val(data.order_id11);
                $('#MID_HDFC').val(user_id_val);
                $('#CUST_ID_HDFC').val(user_id_val);

                $('#CONV_CHARGE_HDFC').val(conv11);
                $('#MAIN_AMOUNT_HDFC').val(trans_amt);

                    var full_call = 'index.php/Homepage/pay24Response_coupon'
                $('#WEB_CALLBACK_URL_HDFC').val('https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/'+full_call);

                document.getElementById('btn_pay_hdfc').click();
    				    
    				   	}
    				else{
    					alert('Something Went Wrong.');
                        location.reload();
    				}
    			}
    		}); 
        
        
    }
        </script>

  <script>
    function showOptions( a ){      
      document.getElementById("inputDomain").style.display = "";

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
 
 
  $('#ref_confirmd').change(function() {

        var inputVal = $(this).val(); 
       
                
        // Send an AJAX request to the server
        $.ajax({
            url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/verify_Referral_Dis' ,
            type: 'POST',
            data: { inputValue: inputVal }, 
            success: function(response) {
           
                if(response =='success'){
                    $('#ref_st').html('');
                     $('#ref_std').html('Referral Code Applied');
                     document.getElementById('ref_code_main').value = inputVal ;
                      
                }else{
                     $('#ref_st').html('Invalid Referral Code');
                      $('#ref_std').html('');
                    document.getElementById('ref_code_main').value = '' ;
                }
            }
        });
    });
    
    
 $('#retail_ref').change(function() {

        var inputVal = $(this).val(); 
       
                
        // Send an AJAX request to the server
        $.ajax({
            url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Homepage/verify_Referral_Ret' ,
            type: 'POST',
            data: { inputValue: inputVal }, 
            success: function(response) {
           
                if(response =='success'){
                    $('#ref_rt').html('');
                     $('#ref_str').html('Referral Code Applied');
                     document.getElementById('ref_code_main').value = inputVal ;
                      
                }else{
                     $('#ref_rt').html('Invalid Referral Code');
                      $('#ref_str').html('');
                    document.getElementById('ref_code_main').value = '' ;
                }
            }
        });
    });

         function onlyNumberKey(evt) {
              
            // Only ASCII character in that range allowed
            var ASCIICode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : evt.keyCode
            if (ASCIICode > 31 && (ASCIICode < 48 || ASCIICode > 57))
                return false;
            return true;
        }
        function validatePanNumber(pan) {

            let pannumber = $(pan).val();

            var regex = /[a-zA-z]{5}\d{4}[a-zA-Z]{1}/;

            if (pannumber.match(regex)) {

                alert(" Valid PAN number");

            }

            else {

                alert(" Invalid PAN number");

                $(pan).val(" ");

            }

        }

            $(".flight_form").hide();

    <script>
         /***********start for flight*************/
         
         var jqOld = jQuery.noConflict();
       
        
         jqOld('#depaturedate').datepicker({
            dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy',
            todayHighlight: true,
            minDate: new Date(),
            numberOfMonths: 2,
            autoclose : true,
            
        }).on("change", function() {

            
           
            var depaturedate=$('#depaturedate').val();
            var split=depaturedate.split("/");
            var startdate=new Date(split[2]+"-"+split[1]+"-"+split[0]);
            
            jqOld("#returndate").datepicker("destroy");
             
            jqOld('#returndate').datepicker({
                dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy',
                minDate: startdate,
                numberOfMonths: 2,
                autoclose : true,
            });
            
            jqOld("#returndate").datepicker("setDate", startdate);

            var returndate=$('#returndate').val();
            $('#hidden_returndate').val(returndate);
            jqOld("#returndate").datepicker("setDate", '');

            $('#hidden_depaturedate').val(depaturedate);
            jqOld("#depaturedate").datepicker("setDate", '');
            $('.depaturedate_cls p').remove();
            var depaturedate=$("#hidden_depaturedate").val();
            var split=depaturedate.split('/');
            var depature_date_html='';

            var d = new Date("'"+split[2]+"-"+split[1]+"-"+split[0]+"'");

            depature_date_html+='<p class="blackText fs4 code lineHeight36 mb-0 depaturedate_html">';
            depature_date_html+='<span class="  latoBlack">'+split[0]+'-</span><span>'+split[1]+'-</span>';
            depature_date_html+='<span class="  latoBlack">'+split[2]+'</span>';
            depature_date_html+='</p>';
            depature_date_html+='<p class="code">'+d.toLocaleDateString('default', { weekday: 'long' });+'</p>';
            $('.depaturedate_cls').append(depature_date_html);
            
            if($('#journytype').val()==2)
            {
                $('.returndate_cls p').remove();
                $('.returndiv').addClass('hidden');
                var returndate=$("#hidden_returndate").val();
                var split=returndate.split('/');
                var return_date_html='';
    
                var d = new Date("'"+split[2]+"-"+split[1]+"-"+split[0]+"'");
    
                return_date_html+='<p class="blackText fs4 code lineHeight36 mb-0 depaturedate_html">';
                return_date_html+='<span class="  latoBlack">'+split[0]+'-</span><span>'+split[1]+'-</span>';
                return_date_html+='<span class="  latoBlack">'+split[2]+'</span>';
                return_date_html+='</p>';
                return_date_html+='<p class="code">'+d.toLocaleDateString('default', { weekday: 'long' });+'</p>';
                $('.returndate_cls').append(return_date_html);
                
            }
            
        });

        getMonthName = function (v) {
            var n = ["January", "February", "March", "April", "May", "June", "July", "August", "September", "October", "November", "December"];
            return n[v]
        }

        jqOld("#depaturedate").datepicker("setDate", new Date());
        $('#hidden_depaturedate').val($("#depaturedate").val());
        jqOld("#depaturedate").datepicker("setDate", '');
        
        var depaturedate=$("#hidden_depaturedate").val();
        var split=depaturedate.split('/');

      <script>
      $(document).ready(function(){
          $("#one_way_btn").click(function(){
            $(this).css('background', '#bb2d3b');
            $("#roundtrip_way_btn").css("background","#6c757d");
          });
          $("#roundtrip_way_btn").click(function(){
            $(this).css('background', '#bb2d3b');
            $("#one_way_btn").css("background","#6c757d");
          });
          $(".returndate_cls").click(function(){
            $("#roundtrip_way_btn").css('background', '#bb2d3b');
            $("#one_way_btn").css("background","#6c757d");
          });
        });
         
         
      $("#exchange_btn").on('click', function() {
            $(this).toggleClass("clicked");
            var temp = $(".first-input").val();
            $(".first-input").val($(".second-input").val());
            $(".second-input").val(temp);
        });
        
        
        
        //fetch airport list data
        $('body').on('keyup','#Origin',function(){
            getaiportlist_origin($('#Origin').val());
        });
        
        
        function getaiportlist_origin(keyword){
            
            var ajax_url='https://bitspanindia.com';
             
            $.ajax({
                url: ajax_url+'/B2C/getairportlist',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {keyword:keyword},
                cache: false,
                success: function (data) {
                    $('.originsearchlist').html(data);
                    $('.originsearchlist').removeClass('hidden');
                    $('.originsearchlist li a').addClass('originli');
                },
            });
        }
        
        //origin li click event
        $('body').on('click','.originli',function(){
            $('#hidden_origin').val($(this).text());
            $('#Origin').val($(this).attr('data-code'));
            $('.origin_airport_name').text($(this).text());
            $('.originsearchlist').html('');
            $('.originsearchlist').addClass('hidden');
        });
        
        $('body').on('focus','#Origin',function(){
            $('#Origin').val('');
            $('.origin_airport_name').text('');
            $('.destinationsearchlist').addClass('hidden');
        });
        
        /************for destination textbox ************/
        $('body').on('focus','#Destination',function(){
            $('#Destination').val('');
            $('.destination_airport_name').text('');
            $('.originsearchlist').addClass('hidden');
        });
        
        //fetch airport list data
        $('body').on('keyup','#Destination',function(){
           
            getaiportlist_destination($('#Destination').val());
        });
        
        
        function getaiportlist_destination(keyword){
            
            var ajax_url='https://bitspanindia.com';
            
            $.ajax({
                url: ajax_url+'/B2C/getairportlist',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {keyword:keyword},
                cache: false,
                success: function (data) {
                    $('.destinationsearchlist').html(data);
                    $('.destinationsearchlist').removeClass('hidden');
                    $('.destinationsearchlist li a').addClass('destinationli');
                },
            });
        }
        
        //origin li click event
        $('body').on('click','.destinationli',function(){
            $('#hidden_destination').val($(this).text());
            $('#Destination').val($(this).attr('data-code'));
            $('.destination_airport_name').text($(this).text());
            $('.destinationsearchlist').html('');
            $('.destinationsearchlist').addClass('hidden');
        });
        
        $('body').on('focus','#pax_count',function(){
            $('#pax_cls').modal('show');
        });
        
        $('body').on('click','#btnapplypax',function(){
            var adult=parseInt($('.adultcountcls li a.active').attr('data-val'));
            var child=parseInt($('.childcountcls li a.active').attr('data-val'));
            var infant=parseInt($('.infantcountcls li a.active').attr('data-val'));
            var total=adult+child+infant;
        
            var fightclass=$('.flightcls li a.active').text();
            $('#pax_count').val(total+" Traveller | "+fightclass);
            $('.total_travcls').text(total);
            $('.flightclass_cls').text(fightclass);
            $('#pax_cls').modal('hide');
        });
        
        
        
        $('body').on('submit','#submitonewayForm',function(){
            
            
            if($('#Origin').val() && $('#Destination').val())
            {
                if($('#Origin').val() != $('#Destination').val())
                {
                    var adult=parseInt($('.adultcountcls li a.active').attr('data-val'));
                    var child=parseInt($('.childcountcls li a.active').attr('data-val'));
                    var infant=parseInt($('.infantcountcls li a.active').attr('data-val'));
                    var total=adult+child+infant;
                    var journytype=$('#submitonewayForm #journytype').val();
                    var Origin=$('#submitonewayForm #Origin').val();
                    var Origin_fullname=$("#submitonewayForm #hidden_origin").val();
        
                    var Destination=$("#submitonewayForm #Destination").val();
                    var Destination_fullname=$("#submitonewayForm #hidden_destination").val();
        
                    var depaturedate=$('#submitonewayForm #hidden_depaturedate').val();
                    var returndate=$('#submitonewayForm #hidden_returndate').val();
        
                    if(total > 0)
                    {
                        var fightclass=$('.flightcls li a.active').attr('data-val') | 1;
                                 
                        $('.progressbarmain_div').removeClass('hidden');
                        $('.progressbarmain_div').addClass('show');
        
                        if(parseInt(journytype)==1)
                        {
                            
                            var tbldata='';
                            tbldata+='<div class="col-md-8">';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Origin : </b>'+$("#submitonewayForm #hidden_origin").val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Destination : </b>'+$("#submitonewayForm #hidden_destination").val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Preferred Departure Date : </b>'+$('#submitonewayForm #hidden_depaturedate').val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='</div>';
                            
                            tbldata+='<div class="col-md-4">';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Adult Count : </b>'+adult+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Child Count : </b>'+child+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Infant Count : </b>'+infant+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='</div>';
        
                            $('.flight_resultdiv').remove();
                            $('.progressbar_detail_cls').html(tbldata);
            
                            ajax_url='https://bitspanindia.com';
                            
                            $.ajax({
                            url: ajax_url+'/B2C/onewaysearchflight_list',
                            type: 'POST',
                            data: {
                                Origin:Origin,
                                Origin_fullname:Origin_fullname,
                                Destination:Destination,
                                Destination_fullname:Destination_fullname,
                                depaturedate:depaturedate,
                                depaturetime:0,
                                faretype:2,
                                AdultCount:adult,
                                ChildCount:child,
                                InfantCount:infant,
                                FlightCabinClass:fightclass,
                            },
                            cache: false,
                            datatype:'json',
                            success: function (data) {
                                    var json = JSON.stringify(data);
                                    var resultdata=JSON.parse(json);
                                    if(resultdata.status==0)
                                    {
                                        window.location.href=ajax_url+"/B2C/OnewayResult";
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        $('.progressbarmain_div .processing').html('');
                                        $('.progressbarmain_div .waitmsg').html('');
                                        $('.progressbarmain_div .progressbar_detail_cls').append('<p class="error text-center">Error : '+resultdata.message+'</p>');
                                    }
                                    
                                },
                            });
                            
                        }
                        else if(parseInt(journytype)==2)
                        {
                            var tbldata='';
                            tbldata+='<div class="col-md-8">';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Origin : </b>'+$("#submitonewayForm #hidden_origin").val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Destination : </b>'+$("#submitonewayForm #hidden_destination").val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Preferred Departure Date : </b>'+$('#submitonewayForm #hidden_depaturedate').val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Preferred Return Date : </b>'+$('#submitonewayForm #hidden_returndate').val()+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='</div>';
                            
                            tbldata+='<div class="col-md-4">';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Adult Count : </b>'+adult+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Child Count : </b>'+child+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='<p><b>Infant Count : </b>'+infant+'</p>';
                            tbldata+='</div>';
        
                            $('.flight_resultdiv').remove();
                            $('.progressbar_detail_cls').html(tbldata);
                            
                            var ajax_url='https://bitspanindia.com';
                            
                            $.ajax({
                            url: ajax_url+'/B2C/Returnsearchflight_list',
                            type: 'POST',
                            data: {
                                Origin:Origin,
                                Origin_fullname:Origin_fullname,
                                Destination:Destination,
                                Destination_fullname:Destination_fullname,
                                depaturedate:depaturedate,
                                depaturetime:0,
                                returndate:returndate,
                                returntime:0,
                                faretype:2,
                                AdultCount:adult,
                                ChildCount:child,
                                InfantCount:infant,
                                FlightCabinClass:fightclass,
                            },
                            cache: false,
                            datatype:'json',
                            success: function (data) {
                                    var json = JSON.stringify(data);
                                    var resultdata=JSON.parse(json);
                                    if(resultdata.status==0)
                                    {
                                        window.location.href=ajax_url+"/B2C/ReturnResult";
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        $('.progressbarmain_div .processing').html('');
                                        $('.progressbarmain_div .waitmsg').html('');
                                        $('.progressbarmain_div .progressbar_detail_cls').append('<p class="error text-center">Error : '+resultdata.message+'</p>');
                                    }
                                    
                                },
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        notif({
                            msg:"<b>Error:</b>Please Select Travellers",
                            type:"error"
                        });
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    notif({
                        msg:"<b>Error:</b>Origin and destination same not allowed",
                        type:"error"
                    });
                }
            }
            else
            {
                notif({
                    msg:"<b>Error:</b>Please select origin or destination from the selection list.",
                    type:"error"
                });
            }
        });
        
        
        
        $('body').on('click','.depaturedate_cls',function(){
                $('#depaturedate').focus();
            });
        
        
            $('body').on('click','.returndate_cls',function(){
                $('#returndate').focus();
            });

    </script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
    var jq = jQuery.noConflict(true);
    jq(document).ready(function() {
     jq('.sub_btn').click(function(event){//alert("test");
      event.preventDefault();
     
       var city = $('#hotel_city').val();
        if (city.length == ""){
             $("#usercity").html("City Can't be Empty");
             return false;
        }
      
      var nights = $('#nights').val();
       if (nights<=0){
             $("#usernight").html("Invalid No.of Nights ");
             return false;
        }
      
      var checkin = $('#checkin').val();
      var checkout = $('#checkout').val();
      
      if (checkout < checkin) {
          $("#userckout").html("Invalid Checkout date ");
          return false;
        }
      
      var nationality = $('#nationality').val();
      var rooms = $('#rooms').val();
      var adults = $('#adults').val();
      var children = $('#children').val();
      //var starrating = $('#starrating').val();
      var starrating = "0-5";
      var rooms = $('#rooms').val();
      var roomguestArr = [];
      var datascountguestArr=[];
    
       //alert(rooms);
        for(var j=1;j<=rooms;j++){
        var datascountguest=[];   
        var datas = [];
        $(".roomguest"+j).each(function () {
         datas.push($(this).val());
        });
       roomguestArr.push(datas);
      
        $(".countguest"+j).each(function () {
         datascountguest.push($(this).val());
        });
        datascountguestArr.push(datascountguest);
    }
    //alert(datascountguest);
    //console.log(datascountguestArr);
    roomguest = JSON.stringify(roomguestArr);
    
    //alert(datascountguestArr.length);
    var guestcnt = 0;
    //alert('old gg:'+datascountguestArr);
    for (var n = 0; n < datascountguestArr.length; n++) {
       // alert('new:'+datascountguestArr[n]);
        for (var m = 0; m < datascountguestArr[n].length; m++) {
        guestcnt += parseFloat(datascountguestArr[n][m]);
        }
    }
    
    //alert('Final count:'+guestcnt);
    
    
    //console.log(roomguest);
      
     
      $('#chkinreq').text(checkin);
      $('#chkroom').text(rooms);
      $('#chkoutreq').text(checkout);
        if(starrating=='0-5')var star='Show All';
      else if(starrating=='0-1')var star='1 Star or less';
      else if(starrating=='0-2')var star='2 Star or less';
      else if(starrating=='0-3')var star='3 Star or less';
      else if(starrating=='0-4')var star='4 Star or less';
      else if(starrating=='0-5')var star='5 Star or less';
      else if(starrating=='1-5')var star='1 Star or more';
      else if(starrating=='2-5')var star='2 Star or more';
      else if(starrating=='3-5')var star='3 Star or more';
      else if(starrating=='4-5')var star='4 Star or more';
      //else if(starrating=='5-5')var star='5 Star or more';
    $('#chkstar').text(star);
      $('#chkgst').text(guestcnt);
      $('#location').text(city);
      
     
      var datastring = "city="+city+"&checkin="+checkin+"&checkout="+checkout+"&nights="+nights+"&nationality="+nationality
              +"&rooms="+rooms+"&adults="+adults+"&children="+children+"&starrating="+starrating+"&roomguest="+roomguest;
      //alert(datastring);
     $('#traveller').modal('hide'); 
     $('#myModal_progress').modal('show');
     
     var ajax_url='https://bitspanindia.com';
     
     $.ajax({
       type:"POST",
       url: ajax_url+"/B2C/Hotel/Hotel/hotel_result_response",
       dataType:"json",
       data: datastring,
      // contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
       success: function(data){
          // alert("success");
           if(data!='Successfully get all Hotels'){
               $('#myModal_progress #errmsg').text('Error:'+data);
               $('#pls').html('');
               $('#load').html('');
           }
           else{
                window.location.href = ajax_url+'/B2C/Hotel/Hotel/hotel_result';
            }
         
       },
       error: function(){
        // alert("Error");
       }
      });
      //}
    /*else {
        $("#usercheck").html("City Can't be Emptydf");
          return false;
        }*/
    });
    
    });
    </script>
    
    <script>
    //$(function() { 
    $(document).ready(function() {
    
    jqOld( "#checkin" ).datepicker({
         onSelect: function(dateText, inst) {
      var checkin = $('#checkin').val();
      //var nights = $('#nights').val();
      var nights = "1";
      var bb = $('#checkin').val();
      var date = new Date(bb);
    
      date.setDate(date.getDate() + (+nights));
    
      var dd = date.getDate();
      if(dd>10){dd=dd}else{dd='0'+dd}
      var mm = date.getMonth() + 1;
      if(mm>10){mm=mm}else{mm='0'+mm}
      var y = date.getFullYear();
      var someFormattedDate = y + '-' + mm + '-' + dd;
      $('#checkout').val(someFormattedDate);
      
      },
      dateFormat: "yy-mm-dd",
      minDate: 0,
      numberOfMonths: 2
      
    });
    jqOld( "#checkout" ).datepicker({
      onSelect: function(dateText, inst) {
      var checkin = $('#checkin').val();
      var checkout = $('#checkout').val();
      var date1 = new Date(checkin);
      var date2 = new Date(checkout);
      var diff = new Date(date2 - date1);
      var days = diff/1000/60/60/24;
      //alert(checkin+'---'+checkout+'---'+diff+'--'+days);
      $('#nights').val(days);
      },
    
      dateFormat: "yy-mm-dd",
      minDate: 0,
      numberOfMonths: 2
    });
    });

    <script>
    function dynamicRoom(noofrooms){
        //alert(noofrooms);
        var i;
        $("#appendnewrow").html('');
             for(i=1;i<=noofrooms;i++)
            {
                $("#appendnewrow").append("<div class=\"row\" id=\"appendnewrow"+i+"\" >\n\
                                            <div class=\"col-md-3 ps-2\" id=\"multileadults"+i+"\"><label class=\"form-label\">Adults(18+)</label><select class=\"form-select countguest"+i+" roomguest"+i+"\" name=\"adults\" id=\"adults\" onchange=\"dynamicChildren(this.value)\" required>\n\
    <option value=\"1\">1</option><option value=\"2\">2</option><option value=\"3\">3</option><option value=\"4\">4</option><option value=\"5\">5</option><option value=\"6\">6</option></select></div>\n\
    <div class=\"col-md-3 ps-2\" id=\"multiplechildren"+i+"\"><label class=\"form-label\">Children((0-12 yrs))</label><select class=\"form-select countguest"+i+" roomguest"+i+"\" name=\"children\" id=\"children\" onchange=\"dynamicChildren(this.value,"+i+")\" required>\n\
    <option selected=\"0\">0</option><option value=\"1\">1</option><option value=\"2\">2</option><option value=\"3\">3</option><option value=\"4\">4</option></select></div>\n\
    <div class=\"col-md-6 ps-2 d-flex gap-2\" id=\"multiplechildrenage"+i+"\"></div>");
            }
                
    }
       
         
    
    function dynamicChildren(noofchild,location){
       //alert(location); 
       var i;
        $("#multiplechildrenage"+location).html(" ");
       
        for(i=1;i<=noofchild;i++)
            {
              //  alert(location);
               $("#multiplechildrenage"+location).append("<div><label class=\"form-label\">Age ?(1-12)</label><select class=\"form-select roomguest"+location+"\" name=\"children\" id=\"children\"  required><option value=\"1\">1</option><option value=\"2\">2</option><option value=\"3\">3</option><option value=\"4\">4</option><option value=\"5\">5</option><option value=\"6\">6</option>\n\
    <option value=\"7\">7</option><option value=\"8\">8</option><option value=\"9\">9</option><option value=\"10\">10</option><option value=\"11\">11</option><option value=\"12\">12</option></select></div></div>");
                
            } 
           
            
            
    }
    </script>

    <script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $("#submitBusForm").submit(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault(); // prevent default form submission
    
            var origin = $('#city_origin').val();
            var destination = $('#city_dest').val();
            var departure_date = $('#bus_date').val();    
            
           
            if(origin=='')
            {
                $('#error').html('Origin cannot be blank.');
            }
            else if(destination=='')
            {
    
                $('#error').html('Destination cannot be blank.');
    
            }
    
            else if(departure_date=='')
            {
    
            $('#error').html('Date cannot be blank.');
    
            }
    
            else if (origin != destination) {  
            
                $("#bus_search").hide();
                $(".flight_resultdiv").hide();
                $(".busprogressbarmain_div").show();
                $('.busprogressbar_detail_cls').html('<p>Origin: ' + origin + '</p><p>Destination: ' + destination + '</p><p>Departure date: ' + departure_date + '</p>');
                $('.busprogressbar_detail_cls').css('text-align', 'center');
    
                var startTime = Date.now();
                var endTime = startTime + (2 * 60 * 1000);
    
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                    var currentTime = Date.now();
                    var remainingTime = endTime - currentTime;
    
                    // Update the dots
                    var dots = $('.dots span');
                    var index = Math.floor((currentTime % 6000) / 1000);
                    dots.css('opacity', 0.2);
                    dots.eq(index).css('opacity', 1);
    
                    // Check if the progress bar is complete
                    if (currentTime >= endTime) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        $('.dots span').css('opacity', 1);
                    }
                }, 1000);
                
               
                var split=departure_date.split('-');
                
                var formate_departure_date = split[2]+"-"+split[1]+"-"+split[0];
            
            
                $.ajax({
                    url: 'https://bitspanindia.com/WL-CNT/main/index.php/Bus/bus_result',
                    type: 'POST',
                    data: {
                        city_origin:origin,
                        city_dest:destination,
                        bus_date:formate_departure_date
                    },
                    cache: false,
                    datatype:'json',
                    success: function (response) {                    
                        var data = JSON.parse(response);                         
                        var message=data.errormess;                   
                        if(data.status==1)
                        {
                            window.location.href=data.redirect_url;
                            
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            $('#api_error').html(message);
                            $('.api_error').css({
                                'text-align': 'center',
                                'color': 'red'
                            });
    
                        }
                        
                    },
                });
    
            //    
    
            } else {
                $('#error').html('Origin and destination cannot be the same.');
    
            } 
            
    
            
        });
    });
    
    
    </script>
